\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+MANBRIEF\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+ graph management functions of the CUDA runtime API (\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+CURRENT\+\_\+\+FILE\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+) \+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+ENDMANBRIEF\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+

This section describes the graph management functions of CUDA runtime application programming interface.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddChildGraphNode()}{cudaGraphAddChildGraphNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Child\+Graph\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{child\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a child graph node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new node which executes an embedded graph, and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

If {\ttfamily h\+Graph} contains allocation or free nodes, this call will return an error.

The node executes an embedded child graph. The child graph is cloned in this call.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em p\+Dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em child\+Graph} & -\/ The graph to clone into this node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddDependencies()}{cudaGraphAddDependencies()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Dependencies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{from,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{to,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Adds dependency edges to a graph. 

The number of dependencies to be added is defined by {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} Elements in {\ttfamily p\+From} and {\ttfamily p\+To} at corresponding indices define a dependency. Each node in {\ttfamily p\+From} and {\ttfamily p\+To} must belong to {\ttfamily graph}.

If {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} is 0, elements in {\ttfamily p\+From} and {\ttfamily p\+To} will be ignored. Specifying an existing dependency will return an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to which dependencies are added \\
\hline
{\em from} & -\/ Array of nodes that provide the dependencies \\
\hline
{\em to} & -\/ Array of dependent nodes \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies to be added\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cudaGraphAddEmptyNode@{cudaGraphAddEmptyNode}}
\index{cudaGraphAddEmptyNode@{cudaGraphAddEmptyNode}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddEmptyNode()}{cudaGraphAddEmptyNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Empty\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates an empty node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new node which performs no operation, and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

An empty node performs no operation during execution, but can be used for transitive ordering. For example, a phased execution graph with 2 groups of n nodes with a barrier between them can be represented using an empty node and 2\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}n dependency edges, rather than no empty node and n\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}2 dependency edges.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Event\+Record\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaa20877ae287175ecb9bd358a4daabe8d}{cuda\+Event\+\_\+t}}}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates an event record node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new event record node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and event specified in {\ttfamily event}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

Each launch of the graph will record {\ttfamily event} to capture execution of the node\textquotesingle{}s dependencies.

These nodes may not be used in loops or conditionals.

{\em event} & -\/ Event for the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Event\+Wait\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaa20877ae287175ecb9bd358a4daabe8d}{cuda\+Event\+\_\+t}}}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates an event wait node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new event wait node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and event specified in {\ttfamily event}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

The graph node will wait for all work captured in {\ttfamily event}. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_v_e_n_t_ga8b5c6177fdc919e456a73684a01d2bac}{cu\+Event\+Record()} for details on what is captured by an event. The synchronization will be performed efficiently on the device when applicable. {\ttfamily event} may be from a different context or device than the launch stream.

These nodes may not be used in loops or conditionals.

{\em ph\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\

{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em event} & -\/ Event for the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_external_semaphore_signal_node_params}{cuda\+External\+Semaphore\+Signal\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates an external semaphore signal node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new external semaphore signal node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

Performs a signal operation on a set of externally allocated semaphore objects when the node is launched. The operation(s) will occur after all of the node\textquotesingle{}s dependencies have completed.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+External\+Semaphores\+Wait\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_external_semaphore_wait_node_params}{cuda\+External\+Semaphore\+Wait\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates an external semaphore wait node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new external semaphore wait node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

Performs a wait operation on a set of externally allocated semaphore objects when the node is launched. The node\textquotesingle{}s dependencies will not be launched until the wait operation has completed.

{\em node\+Params} & -\/ Parameters for the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Host\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_host_node_params}{cuda\+Host\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a host execution node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new CPU execution node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

When the graph is launched, the node will invoke the specified CPU function. Host nodes are not supported under MPS with pre-\/\+Volta GPUs.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{cudaGraphAddKernelNode@{cudaGraphAddKernelNode}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddKernelNode()}{cudaGraphAddKernelNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Kernel\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params}{cuda\+Kernel\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a kernel execution node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new kernel execution node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

The \doxylink{structcuda_kernel_node_params}{cuda\+Kernel\+Node\+Params} structure is defined as\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params}{cudaKernelNodeParams}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params_afce3df9a6ee0a768a8ca4b985558ca82}{func}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structdim3}{dim3}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params_af31836451650cb520658bb2a741c0795}{gridDim}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{structdim3}{dim3}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params_a8df7b04e23379ff141831f28a860f4ae}{blockDim}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params_a6a5412c4983da848deda394309f6f6ed}{sharedMemBytes}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ **\mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params_aa31f5e45ef1c1cfd1d97d21d2217fadd}{kernelParams}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ **\mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params_a59eb4acdd722e24ceaf670bd2d81e872}{extra}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


When the graph is launched, the node will invoke kernel {\ttfamily func} on a ({\ttfamily grid\+Dim.\+x} x {\ttfamily grid\+Dim.\+y} x {\ttfamily grid\+Dim.\+z}) grid of blocks. Each block contains ({\ttfamily block\+Dim.\+x} x {\ttfamily block\+Dim.\+y} x {\ttfamily block\+Dim.\+z}) threads.

{\ttfamily shared\+Mem} sets the amount of dynamic shared memory that will be available to each thread block.

Kernel parameters to {\ttfamily func} can be specified in one of two ways\+:

1) Kernel parameters can be specified via {\ttfamily kernel\+Params}. If the kernel has N parameters, then {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} needs to be an array of N pointers. Each pointer, from {\ttfamily kernel\+Params}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} to {\ttfamily kernel\+Params}\mbox{[}N-\/1\mbox{]}, points to the region of memory from which the actual parameter will be copied. The number of kernel parameters and their offsets and sizes do not need to be specified as that information is retrieved directly from the kernel\textquotesingle{}s image.

2) Kernel parameters can also be packaged by the application into a single buffer that is passed in via {\ttfamily extra}. This places the burden on the application of knowing each kernel parameter\textquotesingle{}s size and alignment/padding within the buffer. The {\ttfamily extra} parameter exists to allow this function to take additional less commonly used arguments. {\ttfamily extra} specifies a list of names of extra settings and their corresponding values. Each extra setting name is immediately followed by the corresponding value. The list must be terminated with either NULL or CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+END.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad5c11cff5adfa5a69d66829399653532}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+END}, which indicates the end of the {\ttfamily extra} array;
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga36d10d0b40c51372877578a2cffd6acd}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+POINTER}, which specifies that the next value in {\ttfamily extra} will be a pointer to a buffer containing all the kernel parameters for launching kernel {\ttfamily func};
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf339c057cd94562ead93a192e11c17e9}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+SIZE}, which specifies that the next value in {\ttfamily extra} will be a pointer to a size\+\_\+t containing the size of the buffer specified with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga36d10d0b40c51372877578a2cffd6acd}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+POINTER};
\end{DoxyItemize}

The error cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value will be returned if kernel parameters are specified with both {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} and {\ttfamily extra} (i.\+e. both {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} and {\ttfamily extra} are non-\/\+NULL).

The {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} or {\ttfamily extra} array, as well as the argument values it points to, are copied during this call.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Kernels launched using graphs must not use texture and surface references. Reading or writing through any texture or surface reference is undefined behavior. This restriction does not apply to texture and surface objects.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddMemAllocNode()}{cudaGraphAddMemAllocNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Alloc\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_mem_alloc_node_params}{cuda\+Mem\+Alloc\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates an allocation node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new allocation node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em p\+Dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em node\+Params} & -\/ Parameters for the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
When \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gaca64e3dd532cd8ec7fe682c240a7a11f}{cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Alloc\+Node} creates an allocation node, it returns the address of the allocation in {\ttfamily node\+Params.\+dptr}. The allocation\textquotesingle{}s address remains fixed across instantiations and launches.

If the allocation is freed in the same graph, by creating a free node using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_ga1aaeffed4953cb15aa25d954090cbab2}{cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Free\+Node}, the allocation can be accessed by nodes ordered after the allocation node but before the free node. These allocations cannot be freed outside the owning graph, and they can only be freed once in the owning graph.

If the allocation is not freed in the same graph, then it can be accessed not only by nodes in the graph which are ordered after the allocation node, but also by stream operations ordered after the graph\textquotesingle{}s execution but before the allocation is freed.

Allocations which are not freed in the same graph can be freed by\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item passing the allocation to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Free\+Async} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Free};
\item launching a graph with a free node for that allocation; or
\item specifying \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Graph\+Instantiate\+Flag\+Auto\+Free\+On\+Launch} during instantiation, which makes each launch behave as though it called \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Mem\+Free\+Async} for every unfreed allocation.
\end{DoxyItemize}

It is not possible to free an allocation in both the owning graph and another graph. If the allocation is freed in the same graph, a free node cannot be added to another graph. If the allocation is freed in another graph, a free node can no longer be added to the owning graph.

The following restrictions apply to graphs which contain allocation and/or memory free nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Nodes and edges of the graph cannot be deleted.
\item The graph cannot be used in a child node.
\item Only one instantiation of the graph may exist at any point in time.
\item The graph cannot be cloned.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Cudart\+Unloading, cuda\+Error\+Initialization\+Error, cuda\+Error\+Not\+Supported, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Error\+Out\+Of\+Memory} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNode()}{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Memcpy\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DParms}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Copy\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a memcpy node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new memcpy node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

When the graph is launched, the node will perform the memcpy described by {\ttfamily p\+Copy\+Params}. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___m_e_m_o_r_y_ga60a55856b9b01a0620ca1c657debed53}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+D()} for a description of the structure and its restrictions.

Memcpy nodes have some additional restrictions with regards to managed memory, if the system contains at least one device which has a zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access.

\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em p\+Dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em p\+Copy\+Params} & -\/ Parameters for the memory copy\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cudaGraphAddMemcpyNode1D@{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNode1D}}
\index{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNode1D@{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNode1D}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNode1D()}{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNode1D()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Memcpy\+Node1D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a 1D memcpy node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new 1D memcpy node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

When the graph is launched, the node will copy {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. Launching a memcpy node with dst and src pointers that do not match the direction of the copy results in an undefined behavior.

Memcpy nodes have some additional restrictions with regards to managed memory, if the system contains at least one device which has a zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em p\+Dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNodeFromSymbol@{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNodeFromSymbol}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNodeFromSymbol()}{cudaGraphAddMemcpyNodeFromSymbol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Memcpy\+Node\+From\+Symbol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a memcpy node to copy from a symbol on the device and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new memcpy node to copy from {\ttfamily symbol} and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

When the graph is launched, the node will copy {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily offset} bytes from the start of symbol {\ttfamily symbol} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily symbol} is a variable that resides in global or constant memory space. {\ttfamily kind} can be either cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing.

Memcpy nodes have some additional restrictions with regards to managed memory, if the system contains at least one device which has a zero value for the device attribute cuda\+Dev\+Attr\+Concurrent\+Managed\+Access.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em p\+Dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em symbol} & -\/ Device symbol address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em offset} & -\/ Offset from start of symbol in bytes \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Free\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a memory free node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new memory free node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} and address specified in {\ttfamily dptr}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em p\+Dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em dptr} & -\/ Address of memory to free\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_ga1aaeffed4953cb15aa25d954090cbab2}{cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Free\+Node} will return cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value if the user attempts to free\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item an allocation twice in the same graph.
\item an address that was not returned by an allocation node.
\item an invalid address.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following restrictions apply to graphs which contain allocation and/or memory free nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Nodes and edges of the graph cannot be deleted.
\item The graph cannot be used in a child node.
\item Only one instantiation of the graph may exist at any point in time.
\item The graph cannot be cloned.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Cudart\+Unloading, cuda\+Error\+Initialization\+Error, cuda\+Error\+Not\+Supported, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Error\+Out\+Of\+Memory} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphAddMemsetNode()}{cudaGraphAddMemsetNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Add\+Memset\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memset_params}{cuda\+Memset\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Memset\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a memset node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new memset node and adds it to {\ttfamily graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Node}.

The element size must be 1, 2, or 4 bytes. When the graph is launched, the node will perform the memset described by {\ttfamily p\+Memset\+Params}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em p\+Dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em p\+Memset\+Params} & -\/ Parameters for the memory set\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Device \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphChildGraphNodeGetGraph()}{cudaGraphChildGraphNodeGetGraph()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Child\+Graph\+Node\+Get\+Graph (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Gets a handle to the embedded graph of a child graph node. 

Gets a handle to the embedded graph in a child graph node. This call does not clone the graph. Changes to the graph will be reflected in the node, and the node retains ownership of the graph.

Allocation and free nodes cannot be added to the returned graph. Attempting to do so will return an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em node} & -\/ Node to get the embedded graph for \\
\hline
{\em p\+Graph} & -\/ Location to store a handle to the graph\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphClone()}{cudaGraphClone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Clone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Clone,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{original\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Clones a graph. 

This function creates a copy of {\ttfamily original\+Graph} and returns it in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Clone}. All parameters are copied into the cloned graph. The original graph may be modified after this call without affecting the clone.

Child graph nodes in the original graph are recursively copied into the clone.

{\em p\+Graph\+Clone} & -\/ Returns newly created cloned graph \\

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphDebugDotPrint()}{cudaGraphDebugDotPrint()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Debug\+Dot\+Print (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{char}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Write a DOT file describing graph structure. 

Using the provided {\ttfamily graph}, write to {\ttfamily path} a DOT formatted description of the graph. By default this includes the graph topology, node types, node id, kernel names and memcpy direction. {\ttfamily flags} can be specified to write more detailed information about each node type such as parameter values, kernel attributes, node and function handles.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em graph} & -\/ The graph to create a DOT file from \\
\hline
{\em path} & -\/ The path to write the DOT file to \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Flags from cuda\+Graph\+Debug\+Dot\+Flags for specifying which additional node information to write\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, cuda\+Error\+Operating\+System 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphDestroyNode()}{cudaGraphDestroyNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Destroy\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Remove a node from the graph. 

Removes {\ttfamily node} from its graph. This operation also severs any dependencies of other nodes on {\ttfamily node} and vice versa.

Dependencies cannot be removed from graphs which contain allocation or free nodes. Any attempt to do so will return an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em node} & -\/ Node to remove\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+destroy\+\_\+ub
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_ga5e8354b1d90d8b1844275a968ce6b179}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_ga5e8354b1d90d8b1844275a968ce6b179} 
\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cudaGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams@{cudaGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams}}
\index{cudaGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams@{cudaGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams()}{cudaGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Child\+Graph\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{child\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Updates node parameters in the child graph node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though the nodes contained in {\ttfamily node\textquotesingle{}s} graph had the parameters contained in {\ttfamily child\+Graph\textquotesingle{}s} nodes at instantiation. {\ttfamily node} must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from {\ttfamily node} are ignored.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily node} is also not modified by this call.

The topology of {\ttfamily child\+Graph}, as well as the node insertion order, must match that of the graph contained in {\ttfamily node}. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gabdd97d722209896183499dab6c66554a}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update()} for a list of restrictions on what can be updated in an instantiated graph. The update is recursive, so child graph nodes contained within the top level child graph will also be updated.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em node} & -\/ Host node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em child\+Graph} & -\/ The graph supplying the updated parameters\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_external_semaphore_signal_node_params}{cuda\+External\+Semaphore\+Signal\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Sets the parameters for an external semaphore signal node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Sets the parameters of an external semaphore signal node in an executable graph {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated.

{\ttfamily h\+Node} must not have been removed from the original graph.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily h\+Node} is also not modified by this call.

Changing {\ttfamily node\+Params-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}num\+Ext\+Sems} is not supported.

{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ semaphore signal node from the graph from which graph\+Exec was instantiated \\
\hline
{\em node\+Params} & -\/ Updated Parameters to set\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

Sets the parameters for a host node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though {\ttfamily node} had contained {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params} at instantiation. {\ttfamily node} must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from {\ttfamily node} are ignored.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily node} is also not modified by this call.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Kernel\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params}{cuda\+Kernel\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Sets the parameters for a kernel node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Sets the parameters of a kernel node in an executable graph {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated.

{\ttfamily node} must not have been removed from the original graph. The {\ttfamily func} field of {\ttfamily node\+Params} cannot be modified and must match the original value. All other values can be modified.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily node} is also not modified by this call.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cudaGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams@{cudaGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams}}
\index{cudaGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams@{cudaGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams()}{cudaGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Memcpy\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memcpy3_d_parms}{cuda\+Memcpy3\+DParms}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Sets the parameters for a memcpy node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though {\ttfamily node} had contained {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params} at instantiation. {\ttfamily node} must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from {\ttfamily node} are ignored.

The source and destination memory in {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params} must be allocated from the same contexts as the original source and destination memory. Both the instantiation-\/time memory operands and the memory operands in {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params} must be 1-\/dimensional. Zero-\/length operations are not supported.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily node} is also not modified by this call.

Returns cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value if the memory operands\textquotesingle{} mappings changed or either the original or new memory operands are multidimensional.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em node} & -\/ Memcpy node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em p\+Node\+Params} & -\/ Updated Parameters to set\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams1D()}{cudaGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams1D()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Memcpy\+Node\+Set\+Params1D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Sets the parameters for a memcpy node in the given graph\+Exec to perform a 1-\/dimensional copy. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though {\ttfamily node} had contained the given params at instantiation. {\ttfamily node} must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from {\ttfamily node} are ignored.

{\ttfamily src} and {\ttfamily dst} must be allocated from the same contexts as the original source and destination memory. The instantiation-\/time memory operands must be 1-\/dimensional. Zero-\/length operations are not supported.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily node} is also not modified by this call.

Returns cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value if the memory operands\textquotesingle{} mappings changed or the original memory operands are multidimensional.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em node} & -\/ Memcpy node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Memcpy\+Node\+Set\+Params\+To\+Symbol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Sets the parameters for a memcpy node in the given graph\+Exec to copy to a symbol on the device. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though {\ttfamily node} had contained the given params at instantiation. {\ttfamily node} must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from {\ttfamily node} are ignored.

{\ttfamily src} and {\ttfamily symbol} must be allocated from the same contexts as the original source and destination memory. The instantiation-\/time memory operands must be 1-\/dimensional. Zero-\/length operations are not supported.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily node} is also not modified by this call.

Returns cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value if the memory operands\textquotesingle{} mappings changed or the original memory operands are multidimensional.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em node} & -\/ Memcpy node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em symbol} & -\/ Device symbol address \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em offset} & -\/ Offset from start of symbol in bytes \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphExecMemsetNodeSetParams()}{cudaGraphExecMemsetNodeSetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Memset\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_memset_params}{cuda\+Memset\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Sets the parameters for a memset node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though {\ttfamily node} had contained {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params} at instantiation. {\ttfamily node} must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from {\ttfamily node} are ignored.

The destination memory in {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params} must be allocated from the same context as the original destination memory. Both the instantiation-\/time memory operand and the memory operand in {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params} must be 1-\/dimensional. Zero-\/length operations are not supported.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily node} is also not modified by this call.

Returns cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value if the memory operand\textquotesingle{}s mappings changed or either the original or new memory operand are multidimensional.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em node} & -\/ Memset node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em p\+Node\+Params} & -\/ Updated Parameters to set\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
