\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gabdd97d722209896183499dab6c66554a}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gabdd97d722209896183499dab6c66554a} 
\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cudaGraphExecUpdate@{cudaGraphExecUpdate}}
\index{cudaGraphExecUpdate@{cudaGraphExecUpdate}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphExecUpdate()}{cudaGraphExecUpdate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga51613142e9be08357296fbd014f77fb0}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Result}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{update\+Result\+\_\+out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Check whether an executable graph can be updated with a graph and perform the update if possible. 

Updates the node parameters in the instantiated graph specified by {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} with the node parameters in a topologically identical graph specified by {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.

Limitations\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Kernel nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The owning context of the function cannot change.
\item A node whose function originally did not use CUDA dynamic parallelism cannot be updated to a function which uses CDP.
\item A cooperative node cannot be updated to a non-\/cooperative node, and vice-\/versa.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Memset and memcpy nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The CUDA device(s) to which the operand(s) was allocated/mapped cannot change.
\item The source/destination memory must be allocated from the same contexts as the original source/destination memory.
\item Only 1D memsets can be changed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Additional memcpy node restrictions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Changing either the source or destination memory type(i.\+e. CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE, CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY, etc.) is not supported.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Note\+: The API may add further restrictions in future releases. The return code should always be checked.

cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update sets {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} to cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error\+Topology\+Changed under the following conditions\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The count of nodes directly in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} and {\ttfamily h\+Graph} differ, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is NULL.
\item A node is deleted in {\ttfamily h\+Graph} but not not its pair from {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is NULL.
\item A node is deleted in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} but not its pair from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is the pairless node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.
\item The dependent nodes of a pair differ, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update sets {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} to\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error if passed an invalid value.
\item cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error\+Topology\+Changed if the graph topology changed
\item cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error\+Node\+Type\+Changed if the type of a node changed, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.
\item cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error\+Function\+Changed if the function of a kernel node changed (CUDA driver \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 11.\+2)
\item cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error\+Unsupported\+Function\+Change if the func field of a kernel changed in an unsupported way(see note above), in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph} 
\item cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error\+Parameters\+Changed if any parameters to a node changed in a way that is not supported, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph} 
\item cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error\+Attributes\+Changed if any attributes of a node changed in a way that is not supported, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph} 
\item cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error\+Not\+Supported if something about a node is unsupported, like the node\textquotesingle{}s type or configuration, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

If {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} isn\textquotesingle{}t set in one of the situations described above, the update check passes and cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update updates {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} to match the contents of {\ttfamily h\+Graph}. If an error happens during the update, {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} will be set to cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Error; otherwise, {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} is set to cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Success.

cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Update returns cuda\+Success when the updated was performed successfully. It returns cuda\+Error\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Failure if the graph update was not performed because it included changes which violated constraints specific to instantiated graph update.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & The instantiated graph to be updated \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & The graph containing the updated parameters \\
\hline
{\em h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} & The node which caused the permissibility check to forbid the update, if any \\
\hline
{\em update\+Result\+\_\+out} & Whether the graph update was permitted. If was forbidden, the reason why\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Graph\+Exec\+Update\+Failure, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node\+Get\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_external_semaphore_signal_node_params}{cuda\+External\+Semaphore\+Signal\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{params\+\_\+out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns an external semaphore signal node\textquotesingle{}s parameters. 

Returns the parameters of an external semaphore signal node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}. The {\ttfamily ext\+Sem\+Array} and {\ttfamily params\+Array} returned in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}, are owned by the node. This memory remains valid until the node is destroyed or its parameters are modified, and should not be modified directly. Use \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gac8cf2dbdf9a62c946ce1c802c29b03f4}{cuda\+Graph\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node\+Set\+Params} to update the parameters of this node.

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns an external semaphore wait node\textquotesingle{}s parameters. 

Returns the parameters of an external semaphore wait node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}. The {\ttfamily ext\+Sem\+Array} and {\ttfamily params\+Array} returned in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}, are owned by the node. This memory remains valid until the node is destroyed or its parameters are modified, and should not be modified directly. Use \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gac8cf2dbdf9a62c946ce1c802c29b03f4}{cuda\+Graph\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node\+Set\+Params} to update the parameters of this node.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node to get the parameters for \\
\hline
{\em params\+\_\+out} & -\/ Pointer to return the parameters\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Get\+Edges (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{from,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{to,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{num\+Edges }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns a graph\textquotesingle{}s dependency edges. 

Returns a list of {\ttfamily graph\textquotesingle{}s} dependency edges. Edges are returned via corresponding indices in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to}; that is, the node in {\ttfamily to}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} has a dependency on the node in {\ttfamily from}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]}. {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} may both be NULL, in which case this function only returns the number of edges in {\ttfamily num\+Edges}. Otherwise, {\ttfamily num\+Edges} entries will be filled in. If {\ttfamily num\+Edges} is higher than the actual number of edges, the remaining entries in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} will be set to NULL, and the number of edges actually returned will be written to {\ttfamily num\+Edges}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to get the edges from \\
\hline
{\em from} & -\/ Location to return edge endpoints \\
\hline
{\em to} & -\/ Location to return edge endpoints \\
\hline
{\em num\+Edges} & -\/ See description\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns a graph\textquotesingle{}s nodes. 

Returns a list of {\ttfamily graph\textquotesingle{}s} nodes. {\ttfamily nodes} may be NULL, in which case this function will return the number of nodes in {\ttfamily num\+Nodes}. Otherwise, {\ttfamily num\+Nodes} entries will be filled in. If {\ttfamily num\+Nodes} is higher than the actual number of nodes, the remaining entries in {\ttfamily nodes} will be set to NULL, and the number of nodes actually obtained will be returned in {\ttfamily num\+Nodes}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphInstantiate()}{cudaGraphInstantiate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Instantiate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Error\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{char}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Log\+Buffer,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{buffer\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates an executable graph from a graph. 

Instantiates {\ttfamily graph} as an executable graph. The graph is validated for any structural constraints or intra-\/node constraints which were not previously validated. If instantiation is successful, a handle to the instantiated graph is returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Exec}.

If there are any errors, diagnostic information may be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Error\+Node} and {\ttfamily p\+Log\+Buffer}. This is the primary way to inspect instantiation errors. The output will be null terminated unless the diagnostics overflow the buffer. In this case, they will be truncated, and the last byte can be inspected to determine if truncation occurred.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ Returns instantiated graph \\
\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to instantiate \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Node} & -\/ In case of an instantiation error, this may be modified to indicate a node contributing to the error \\
\hline
{\em p\+Log\+Buffer} & -\/ A character buffer to store diagnostic messages \\
\hline
{\em buffer\+Size} & -\/ Size of the log buffer in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphInstantiateWithFlags()}{cudaGraphInstantiateWithFlags()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Instantiate\+With\+Flags (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{long}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{long}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates an executable graph from a graph. 

Instantiates {\ttfamily graph} as an executable graph. The graph is validated for any structural constraints or intra-\/node constraints which were not previously validated. If instantiation is successful, a handle to the instantiated graph is returned in {\ttfamily p\+Graph\+Exec}.

The {\ttfamily flags} parameter controls the behavior of instantiation and subsequent graph launches. Valid flags are\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Graph\+Instantiate\+Flag\+Auto\+Free\+On\+Launch}, which configures a graph containing memory allocation nodes to automatically free any unfreed memory allocations before the graph is relaunched.
\end{DoxyItemize}

If {\ttfamily graph} contains any allocation or free nodes, there can be at most one executable graph in existence for that graph at a time.

An attempt to instantiate a second executable graph before destroying the first with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_ga681bde989cc3ec1a68d788f3a237ef2b}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+Destroy} will result in an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ Returns instantiated graph \\
\hline
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph to instantiate \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Flags to control instantiation. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabc4dc810c9913d836bf62a7b2be791dd}{CUgraph\+Instantiate\+\_\+flags}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphKernelNodeGetParams()}{cudaGraphKernelNodeGetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Kernel\+Node\+Get\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_kernel_node_params}{cuda\+Kernel\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns a kernel node\textquotesingle{}s parameters. 

Returns the parameters of kernel node {\ttfamily node} in {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params}. The {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} or {\ttfamily extra} array returned in {\ttfamily p\+Node\+Params}, as well as the argument values it points to, are owned by the node. This memory remains valid until the node is destroyed or its parameters are modified, and should not be modified directly. Use \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gae9f5733288ed5046f782b994c16b4d5e}{cuda\+Graph\+Kernel\+Node\+Set\+Params} to update the parameters of this node.

The params will contain either {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} or {\ttfamily extra}, according to which of these was most recently set on the node.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphLaunch()}{cudaGraphLaunch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Launch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}}}]{stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Launches an executable graph in a stream. 

Executes {\ttfamily graph\+Exec} in {\ttfamily stream}. Only one instance of {\ttfamily graph\+Exec} may be executing at a time. Each launch is ordered behind both any previous work in {\ttfamily stream} and any previous launches of {\ttfamily graph\+Exec}. To execute a graph concurrently, it must be instantiated multiple times into multiple executable graphs.

If any allocations created by {\ttfamily graph\+Exec} remain unfreed (from a previous launch) and {\ttfamily graph\+Exec} was not instantiated with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Graph\+Instantiate\+Flag\+Auto\+Free\+On\+Launch}, the launch will fail with cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em graph\+Exec} & -\/ Executable graph to launch \\
\hline
{\em stream} & -\/ Stream in which to launch the graph\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Mem\+Alloc\+Node\+Get\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcuda_mem_alloc_node_params}{cuda\+Mem\+Alloc\+Node\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{params\+\_\+out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns a memory alloc node\textquotesingle{}s parameters. 

Returns the parameters of a memory alloc node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}. The {\ttfamily pool\+Props} and {\ttfamily access\+Descs} returned in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}, are owned by the node. This memory remains valid until the node is destroyed. The returned parameters must not be modified.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Memcpy\+Node\+Set\+Params1D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Sets a memcpy node\textquotesingle{}s parameters to perform a 1-\/dimensional copy. 

Sets the parameters of memcpy node {\ttfamily node} to the copy described by the provided parameters.

When the graph is launched, the node will copy {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}, where {\ttfamily kind} specifies the direction of the copy, and must be one of cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing. Launching a memcpy node with dst and src pointers that do not match the direction of the copy results in an undefined behavior.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em node} & -\/ Node to set the parameters for \\
\hline
{\em dst} & -\/ Destination memory address \\
\hline
{\em src} & -\/ Source memory address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphMemcpyNodeSetParamsFromSymbol()}{cudaGraphMemcpyNodeSetParamsFromSymbol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Memcpy\+Node\+Set\+Params\+From\+Symbol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dst,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{symbol,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{offset,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8ce1ad49a1e77a595edcb25ac795cd0f}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Kind}}}]{kind }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Sets a memcpy node\textquotesingle{}s parameters to copy from a symbol on the device. 

Sets the parameters of memcpy node {\ttfamily node} to the copy described by the provided parameters.

When the graph is launched, the node will copy {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily offset} bytes from the start of symbol {\ttfamily symbol} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily dst}. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily symbol} is a variable that resides in global or constant memory space. {\ttfamily kind} can be either cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Host, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. However, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is only allowed on systems that support unified virtual addressing.

{\em symbol} & -\/ Device symbol address \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ Size in bytes to copy \\
\hline
{\em offset} & -\/ Offset from start of symbol in bytes \\
\hline
{\em kind} & -\/ Type of transfer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

Sets a memcpy node\textquotesingle{}s parameters to copy to a symbol on the device. 

Sets the parameters of memcpy node {\ttfamily node} to the copy described by the provided parameters.

When the graph is launched, the node will copy {\ttfamily count} bytes from the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily src} to the memory area pointed to by {\ttfamily offset} bytes from the start of symbol {\ttfamily symbol}. The memory areas may not overlap. {\ttfamily symbol} is a variable that resides in global or constant memory space. {\ttfamily kind} can be either cuda\+Memcpy\+Host\+To\+Device, cuda\+Memcpy\+Device\+To\+Device, or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default}. Passing \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+Memcpy\+Default} is recommended, in which case the type of transfer is inferred from the pointer values. \doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphNodeFindInClone()}{cudaGraphNodeFindInClone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Find\+In\+Clone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{original\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{cloned\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Finds a cloned version of a node. 

This function returns the node in {\ttfamily cloned\+Graph} corresponding to {\ttfamily original\+Node} in the original graph.

{\ttfamily cloned\+Graph} must have been cloned from {\ttfamily original\+Graph} via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gab67dc1ab9d77726017a6aa4c63686a6d}{cuda\+Graph\+Clone}. {\ttfamily original\+Node} must have been in {\ttfamily original\+Graph} at the time of the call to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_gab67dc1ab9d77726017a6aa4c63686a6d}{cuda\+Graph\+Clone}, and the corresponding cloned node in {\ttfamily cloned\+Graph} must not have been removed. The cloned node is then returned via {\ttfamily p\+Cloned\+Node}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Node} & -\/ Returns handle to the cloned node \\
\hline
{\em original\+Node} & -\/ Handle to the original node \\
\hline
{\em cloned\+Graph} & -\/ Cloned graph to query\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphNodeGetDependencies()}{cudaGraphNodeGetDependencies()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Get\+Dependencies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Num\+Dependencies }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Returns a node\textquotesingle{}s dependencies. 

Returns a list of {\ttfamily node\textquotesingle{}s} dependencies. {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} may be NULL, in which case this function will return the number of dependencies in {\ttfamily p\+Num\+Dependencies}. Otherwise, {\ttfamily p\+Num\+Dependencies} entries will be filled in. If {\ttfamily p\+Num\+Dependencies} is higher than the actual number of dependencies, the remaining entries in {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} will be set to NULL, and the number of nodes actually obtained will be returned in {\ttfamily p\+Num\+Dependencies}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em node} & -\/ Node to query \\
\hline
{\em p\+Dependencies} & -\/ Pointer to return the dependencies \\
\hline
{\em p\+Num\+Dependencies} & -\/ See description\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphNodeGetEnabled()}{cudaGraphNodeGetEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Get\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{is\+Enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Query whether a node in the given graph\+Exec is enabled. 

Sets is\+Enabled to 1 if {\ttfamily h\+Node} is enabled, or 0 if {\ttfamily h\+Node} is disabled.

The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated. ~\newline


{\ttfamily h\+Node} must not have been removed from the original graph.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Currently only kernel nodes are supported.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node from the graph from which graph\+Exec was instantiated \\
\hline
{\em is\+Enabled} & -\/ Location to return the enabled status of the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphNodeSetEnabled()}{cudaGraphNodeSetEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Set\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{is\+Enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Enables or disables the specified node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Sets {\ttfamily h\+Node} to be either enabled or disabled. Disabled nodes are functionally equivalent to empty nodes until they are reenabled. Existing node parameters are not affected by disabling/enabling the node.

The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated. ~\newline


{\ttfamily h\+Node} must not have been removed from the original graph.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily h\+Node} is also not modified by this call.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Currently only kernel nodes are supported.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node from the graph from which graph\+Exec was instantiated \\
\hline
{\em is\+Enabled} & -\/ Node is enabled if != 0, otherwise the node is disabled\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Remove\+Dependencies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gabb3d2a1b44af920c933d053feaa6f5e0}{cuda\+Graph\+\_\+t}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{from,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gafdf0e2bc012d450b895c1d53f7a6fa34}{cuda\+Graph\+Node\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{to,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Removes dependency edges from a graph. 

The number of {\ttfamily p\+Dependencies} to be removed is defined by {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies}. Elements in {\ttfamily p\+From} and {\ttfamily p\+To} at corresponding indices define a dependency. Each node in {\ttfamily p\+From} and {\ttfamily p\+To} must belong to {\ttfamily graph}.

If {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} is 0, elements in {\ttfamily p\+From} and {\ttfamily p\+To} will be ignored. Specifying a non-\/existing dependency will return an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em graph} & -\/ Graph from which to remove dependencies \\
\hline
{\em from} & -\/ Array of nodes that provide the dependencies \\
\hline
{\em to} & -\/ Array of dependent nodes \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies to be removed\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+callback
\end{DoxyReturn}

Retain a reference to a user object from a graph. 

Creates or moves user object references that will be owned by a CUDA graph.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaGraphUpload()}{cudaGraphUpload()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+Graph\+Upload (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga2fee13c408fb7da16401e25c1ae6bdb9}{cuda\+Graph\+Exec\+\_\+t}}}]{graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gae6a6dd5bf3109046a07da4b735234e81}{cuda\+Stream\+\_\+t}}}]{stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Uploads an executable graph in a stream. 

Uploads {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} to the device in {\ttfamily h\+Stream} without executing it. Uploads of the same {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} will be serialized. Each upload is ordered behind both any previous work in {\ttfamily h\+Stream} and any previous launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Uses memory cached by {\ttfamily stream} to back the allocations owned by {\ttfamily graph\+Exec}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ Executable graph to upload \\
\hline
{\em h\+Stream} & -\/ Stream in which to upload the graph\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value, \textbackslash{}notefnerr \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+init\+\_\+rt
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_ga627ee9542b2f32c6d633a0399e4459fe}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___g_r_a_p_h_ga627ee9542b2f32c6d633a0399e4459fe} 
\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cudaUserObjectCreate@{cudaUserObjectCreate}}
\index{cudaUserObjectCreate@{cudaUserObjectCreate}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaUserObjectCreate()}{cudaUserObjectCreate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+User\+Object\+Create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8f6add7500a13a4353bd2249713e3712}{cuda\+User\+Object\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{object\+\_\+out,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gad5a8cb127cd8e78ae1c721e797873110}{cuda\+Host\+Fn\+\_\+t}}}]{destroy,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{initial\+Refcount,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Create a user object. 

Create a user object with the specified destructor callback and initial reference count. The initial references are owned by the caller.

Destructor callbacks cannot make CUDA API calls and should avoid blocking behavior, as they are executed by a shared internal thread. Another thread may be signaled to perform such actions, if it does not block forward progress of tasks scheduled through CUDA.

See CUDA User Objects in the CUDA C++ Programming Guide for more information on user objects.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em object\+\_\+out} & -\/ Location to return the user object handle \\
\hline
{\em ptr} & -\/ The pointer to pass to the destroy function \\
\hline
{\em destroy} & -\/ Callback to free the user object when it is no longer in use \\
\hline
{\em initial\+Refcount} & -\/ The initial refcount to create the object with, typically 1. The initial references are owned by the calling thread. \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Currently it is required to pass \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{cuda\+User\+Object\+No\+Destructor\+Sync}, which is the only defined flag. This indicates that the destroy callback cannot be waited on by any CUDA API. Users requiring synchronization of the callback should signal its completion manually.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaUserObjectRelease()}{cudaUserObjectRelease()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+User\+Object\+Release (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8f6add7500a13a4353bd2249713e3712}{cuda\+User\+Object\+\_\+t}}}]{object,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{count}} }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Release a reference to a user object. 

Releases user object references owned by the caller. The object\textquotesingle{}s destructor is invoked if the reference count reaches zero.

It is undefined behavior to release references not owned by the caller, or to use a user object handle after all references are released.

See CUDA User Objects in the CUDA C++ Programming Guide for more information on user objects.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em object} & -\/ The object to release \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ The number of references to release, typically 1. Must be nonzero and not larger than INT\+\_\+\+MAX.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaUserObjectRetain()}{cudaUserObjectRetain()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+host\+\_\+\+\_\+}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga15962a7f6f36e86b4041cd482f69ff10}{cuda\+Error\+\_\+t}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CUDARTAPI}} cuda\+User\+Object\+Retain (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8f6add7500a13a4353bd2249713e3712}{cuda\+User\+Object\+\_\+t}}}]{object,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{count}} }]{\+\_\+\+\_\+dv1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Retain a reference to a user object. 

Retains new references to a user object. The new references are owned by the caller.

See CUDA User Objects in the CUDA C++ Programming Guide for more information on user objects.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em object} & -\/ The object to retain \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ The number of references to retain, typically 1. Must be nonzero and not larger than INT\+\_\+\+MAX.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
cuda\+Success, cuda\+Error\+Invalid\+Value
\end{DoxyReturn}
